\put(48.66,-115.0997){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}1.1. Health, safety and security of Owners, Occupier of Lots and others }
\put(77.04,-133.4597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must not use the Lot, or permit it to be used, so as to cause a hazard to the }
\put(105.47,-151.636){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}health, safety and security of an Owner, Occupier, or user of another Lot. }
\put(77.04,-170.0597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must not use a Lot or the Common Property for any purpose which may: }
\put(105.42,-188.4197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) be contrary to any Law; }
\put(105.42,-206.5997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) adversely affect the reputation of the Development;  }
\put(105.42,-224.7797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) be reasonably likely to cause or contribute to any loss or damage of a Lot or the Common Property; }
\put(133.7999,-237.0242){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}and }
\put(105.42,-255.3796){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) be reasonably likely to cause or contribute to any nuisance or hazard. }
\put(77.04,-273.7397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must not permit any child under the age of 14 years, and owner whom the }
\put(105.48,-292.0362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owner or Occupier has control, to remain unaccompanied (by a responsible adult) on Common Property, }
\put(105.48,-310.3327){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}including car parking areas and/or recreational areas (if applicable), where there is a hazard or possible }
\put(105.48,-328.6292){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}danger. }
\put(77.04,-346.9997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(4) An Owner or Occupier must, if any infectious disease, which may require notification because of any law, }
\put(105.49,-365.2962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}affects any person in a Lot, give or cause to be given, notice of that fact and any other information which }
\put(105.49,-383.6528){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}may be required about the disease, to the Owners Corporation }
\put(77.04,-402.0197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(5) Further to rule 1.1(4), the Owner must pay to the Owners Corporation the expense of disinfecting the }
\put(105.48,-420.3162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}affected lots (if that is necessary) and replacing any article or thing the destruction of which may be }
\put(105.48,-438.6127){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}rendered necessary by that disease }
\put(48.66,-457.0997){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}1.2. Fire Safety including Emergency Procedures }
\put(77.04,-475.2197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) Obstruction of Exits }
\put(105.48,-493.4561){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must ensure that Common Property and emergency exits from the Building }
\put(105.48,-511.7526){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}or Lots are not obstructed at any time. }
\put(77.04,-530.1197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) Fire Control }
\put(105.42,-548.4196){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) The Owners Corporation may secure and keep the Common Property and any Lots safe from fire or }
\put(133.7999,-566.7161){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}other hazards. This includes: }
\put(133.74,-585.0197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) permanently or temporarily closing off and restricting access to any part of the Common }
\put(162.12,-603.3162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Property not required for access to a Lot; }
\put(133.74,-621.7997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(ii) allowing part of the Common Property to be used for security purposes including monitoring }
\put(162.12,-640.0361){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}security and safety of Lots, even if this means excluding Owners or Occupiers from using that }
\put(162.12,-658.3928){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}part of the Common Property; and }
\put(133.74,-676.6996){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(iii) restrict by means of key or other security device the access of the Owners or Occupiers of one }
\put(162.12,-694.9961){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}level of the Building any other level of the Building. }
\put(105.42,-713.2997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) The Owners Corporation is responsible for the repair and maintenance of the fire safety system for }
\put(133.7999,-731.476){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Development, which includes that part of the system situated within each Lot. }
\put(105.42,-749.8397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must not and they must not permit their invitees to interfere with }
\put(133.7999,-768.1964){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the fire safety system within and around the Development or otherwise behave in a manner that }
\put(133.7999,-786.4929){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}will, does or may cause a false fire alarm resulting in the fire authority attending the building. }
\end{picture}

\put(15,-806.8997){\fontsize{7.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}[8200216: 28038413\_1] }
\put(15,-73.27972){\fontsize{4.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }
\put(105.42,-86.89972){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) Stairwells, electrical riser (service) cupboards and other service cupboards must not be used for any }
\put(133.7999,-105.2563){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}other purpose than that intended. An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must not under any circumstances }
\put(133.8099,-123.5529){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}use these areas, or permit these areas to be used for the storage of goods, waste, cartons etc. }
\put(105.42,-141.7997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) Stairwells must not be obstructed at any time. }
\put(105.42,-160.0997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(f) The door leading to the stairwells and Lots are fire resisting and self-closing. An Owner or Occupier }
\put(133.8099,-178.3962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}of a Lot must ensure that all doors are properly closed and under no circumstances are they to be }
\put(133.8099,-196.7528){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}wedged oped as in the instance of a fire, smoke may penetrate the stairwell and eliminate the }
\put(133.8099,-215.0493){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}effectiveness of the stairwells being used as an escape route. }
\put(105.42,-233.4197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(g) The Owners Corporation, an Owner or Occupier of a Lot, or a representative appointed by the }
\put(133.7999,-251.7162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owners Corporation must not install deadlocks or peep holes that breach the fire regulations }
\put(133.7899,-270.0127){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}set out in Part 7 Division 2 of the Building Regulations 2006 or may void the Owners }
\put(133.7898,-288.3092){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation’s insurance policy. }
\put(105.42,-306.6797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(h) The Owners Corporation, an Owner or Occupier of a Lot, or a representative appointed by the }
\put(133.7999,-324.9762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owners Corporation must, in respect of the Building or the Lot, as appropriate: }
\put(133.74,-343.3397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) consult with any relevant authority as to an appropriate fire alarm and fire sprinkler system }
\put(162.12,-361.6362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}for the Building or the Lot; }
\put(133.74,-379.9397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(ii) ensure the provision of all adequate equipment to prevent fire or the spread of fire in or from }
\put(162.11,-398.2362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Building or the Lot to the satisfaction of all relevant Governmental Agency; }
\put(133.74,-416.5997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(iii) take all reasonable steps to ensure compliance with fire laws in respect of the Building or the }
\put(162.12,-434.776){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Lot; and }
\put(133.74,-453.0797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(iv) not interfere or activate any fire protection services in the Common Property or Building }
\put(162.13,-471.4363){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}including but not limited to alarms, sprinklers, smoke detectors and fire hydrants except in }
\put(162.13,-489.7328){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the case of an emergency. The Owners Corporation may recover the cost of any charges for }
\put(162.13,-508.0294){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}false alarms or making good any damage from the Owner or Occupier for breach of this Rule. }
\put(77.04,-526.5797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) Fire Control Laws }
\put(105.48,-544.6959){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}An Owner or Occupier of a Lot and the Owners Corporation must comply with all laws and requirements of }
\put(105.48,-562.8721){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}relevant authorities on fire prevention and fire control. }
\put(77.04,-581.2397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(4) Fire Drill }
\put(105.48,-599.416){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must: }
\put(105.42,-617.8397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) observe all fire and emergency drills. This includes participating in any building evacuation drills; }
\put(105.42,-636.1997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) ensure that they are aware of all safety and emergency procedures; and }
\put(105.42,-654.5597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) follow the directions of any person who the Owners Corporation nominates as a fire warden to }
\put(133.7999,-672.7961){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}supervise the orderly evacuation of their Lot and the Common Property during any drill or }
\put(133.7999,-691.1527){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}emergency. }
\put(77.04,-709.3997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(5) Emergency Equipment }
\put(105.42,-727.7597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must: }
\put(133.74,-745.9997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) not use or interfere with any fire safety equipment except in the case of any emergency; }
\put(133.74,-764.3596){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(ii) not obstruct any fire stairs or fire escape; }
\put(133.74,-782.6597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(iii) comply with all fire laws in respect of their Lot, including installing all required fire, fighting }
\put(162.13,-800.9562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}equipment and smoke detectors; }
\end{picture}

\put(133.74,-86.89972){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(iv) ensure that all fire safety and other emergency equipment installed in their Lot are properly }
\put(162.12,-105.2563){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}maintained and tested, and that back up batteries for smoke detectors are replaced as }
\put(162.12,-123.5529){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}necessary; }
\put(133.74,-141.8597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(v) immediately notify the Owners Corporation if any fire monitoring or safety equipment }
\put(162.12,-160.0359){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}appears damaged, tampered with or not functioning; }
\put(133.74,-178.3997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(vi) not cause a false fire alarm. If the Owners Corporation incurs a cost from the responsible fire }
\put(162.12,-196.7563){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}authority and/or essential service maintenance contractor because of a false fire alarm, the }
\put(162.13,-215.0529){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owners Corporation may recover the costs from the Owner or Occupier responsible; }
\put(133.74,-233.3597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(vii) ensure that they or their invitees do not open the door to their Lot in non-dangerous }
\put(162.12,-251.6562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}instances such as when smoke or fumes are released from burning food, steam cleaning of }
\put(162.12,-269.9527){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}carpets etc. Only windows should be used in these situations to avoid false alarms and }
\put(162.13,-288.2492){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}unnecessary call outs by the fire authority or other emergency services; and }
\put(133.74,-306.6197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(viii) upon receiving 24 hours’ notice, provide the contractor nominated by the Manager or Owners }
\put(162.12,-324.9162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation, access to their Lot, for the purpose of performing maintenance of the Building’s }
\put(162.12,-343.2127){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}smoke detection and sprinkler system and all essential safety services and devices. }
\put(77.04,-361.5197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(6) Imminent Danger }
\put(105.48,-379.8763){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}If there is a danger or threat concerning their Lot or the Common Property (for example, a bomb threat), an }
\put(105.48,-398.1127){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owner or Occupier of a Lot must immediately: }
\put(105.42,-416.4197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) notify the Manager or the Owners Corporation of the danger or threat; }
\put(105.42,-434.7197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) obey the Manager or the Owners Corporation instructions, including evacuating the Lot or the }
\put(133.7999,-453.0162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Common Property; and }
\put(105.42,-471.5597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) obey the instructions of the policy, fire brigade or relevant Authority. }
\put(48.66,-489.6197){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}1.3. Security }
\put(77.04,-507.9796){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) The Owners Corporation may take measures to ensure the security of the Common Property and any Lots }
\put(105.48,-526.216){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}from fire, floor or other hazards and may (without limitation): }
\put(105.42,-544.5797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) close any part of the Common Property not required as the only access to a Lot or either a }
\put(133.7999,-562.9363){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}temporary or permanent basis or otherwise restrict the access to or use by Owners or Occupiers of }
\put(133.8099,-581.2328){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}any part of the Common Property; }
\put(105.42,-599.5397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) permit any designated part of the Common Property to be used by any security person or }
\put(133.7999,-617.8362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}representative of the Owners Corporation to the exclusion of Occupiers as a means of monitoring }
\put(133.7999,-636.1328){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}security and general safety of any Lot or Common Property, either solely or in conjunction with other }
\put(133.7999,-654.4293){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Lots; }
\put(105.42,-672.7997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) install and operate on the Common Property closed-circuit television monitoring devices, audio- }
\put(133.7999,-691.0962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}visual cameras and other audio-visual surveillance devices to monitor the security, safety and use of }
\put(133.7999,-709.3928){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Common Property and Lots; }
\put(105.42,-727.6996){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) restrict by means of Security Keys, the access of Occupiers to any Common Property; }
\put(105.42,-745.9397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) restrict by means of Security Keys, the access of Occupiers of one level of the Development to any }
\put(133.7999,-764.2963){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}other level of the Development; }
\end{picture}

\put(105.42,-86.83972){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(f) control Security Keys by time periods and enforce use by dates; }
\put(105.42,-105.2597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(g) the right (upon complaint) to remove any person from the Common Property or to refuse admission }
\put(133.7999,-123.436){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}to any person it considers likely to be a nuisance or a security risk; }
\put(105.42,-141.7997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(h) the right of admission to any person subject to limits on the time of use and the parts of Common }
\put(133.7999,-160.0962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}property that may be used or the manner of use and the right to revoke that right of admission at }
\put(133.7999,-178.3927){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}any time on reasonable grounds; and }
\put(105.42,-196.7597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) the Owners Corporation is not liable for and the Owner releases and indemnifies the Owners }
\put(133.7999,-215.0562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation from and against any injury to or death of a person or loss of or damage to property }
\put(133.7999,-233.4128){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(whether in or on Common Property or in or on a lot) arising because: }
\put(133.74,-251.8997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) the security system is not operating; or }
\put(133.74,-269.9597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(ii) the security system fails to operate as intended. }
\put(77.04,-288.3197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must: }
\put(105.42,-306.5597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) comply with any action or direction taken by the Owners Corporation in relation to the security or }
\put(133.7999,-324.8562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}safety of the Common Property and Lots; }
\put(105.42,-343.4597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) ensure that all fire and security doors, gates and other doors are properly closed after use; }
\put(105.42,-361.5797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) not do anything that may interfere with the security or safety of the Common Property or a Lot; }
\put(105.42,-379.9397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) not interfere with any closed-circuit television monitoring devices, audio-visual cameras and }
\put(133.7999,-398.116){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}other audio-visual surveillance devices; and }
\put(105.42,-416.4197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) not to do or permit anything to be done that may prejudice the security or safety of the Common }
\put(133.7999,-434.7763){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Property or any person in or around the Building. }
\put(77.04,-453.0197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) Without limiting the generality of the requirement of Rule 1.3(2)(a), an Owner or Occupier must not: }
\put(105.42,-471.3197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) allow any unknown guest(s) to enter the Building; }
\put(105.42,-489.6797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) allow anyone access to the foyer or car park if they have not used normal security procedures to }
\put(133.7999,-508.0363){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}enter; }
\put(105.42,-526.3397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) allow their guest/invitees to access the Building or use the common area facilities unless they are }
\put(133.8099,-544.6362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}accompanied by an Owner or Occupier of a Lot. }
\put(77.04,-563.1797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(4) All Security Keys remain the property of the individual Owner and an Occupier must: }
\put(105.42,-581.1797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) keep the Security Keys and/or remote control which has been allocated, safe; }
\put(105.42,-599.5397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) immediately report the loss of any Security Key to the Owners Corporation; }
\put(105.42,-617.8997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) immediately noting the Owners Corporation of any person who is not an Owner or Occupier of a Lot }
\put(133.7999,-636.1962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}to whom a Security Key has been made available; }
\put(105.42,-654.7397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) not copy any Security Key; }
\put(105.42,-672.8596){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) ensure that only the Owners Corporation replace any Security Key; }
\put(105.42,-691.2197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(f) pay the Owners Corporation a reasonable fee (determined by the Owners Corporation) for any }
\put(133.7998,-709.396){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}replacement or additional Security Key; }
\put(105.42,-727.7597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(g) comply with the reasonable requirements of the Owners Corporation in relation to Security Keys, }
\put(133.7999,-745.8759){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}including any requirement to limit the number of Security Keys issued in relation to any Lot; and }
\put(105.42,-764.2997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(h) not give or lend any Security Key to someone who is not an Occupier. }

\put(48.66,-86.83972){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}1.4. Storage of flammable liquids and other dangerous substances and materials }
\put(77.04,-105.2597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must not use or store on the Lot (including any accessory Lots) and / or on }
\put(105.48,-123.6163){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Common Property any flammable or noxious chemical, liquid or gas or other flammable or noxious }
\put(105.48,-141.9128){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}material except chemicals, liquids, gases or other material used or intended to be used for domestic }
\put(105.48,-160.2094){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}purposes, or any chemical, liquid, gas or other material in a fuel tank of a motor vehicle or internal }
\put(105.48,-178.5059){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}combustion engine. }
\put(77.04,-196.9997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must only keep any substance permitted under Rule 1.4(1): }
\put(105.42,-215.1197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) at its own risk in all things; and }
\put(105.42,-233.2997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) provided that doing so, does not breach any other Rule. }
\put(48.66,-251.6597){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}1.5. Waste Disposal }
\put(77.04,-270.0197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must ensure that the disposal of garbage or waste does not adversely affect }
\put(105.48,-288.3162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the health, hygiene or comfort of the occupiers or users of other Lots. }
\put(77.04,-306.6797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must: }
\put(105.42,-324.9197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) not deposit, throw, leave or store any rubbish, dirt, dust sweepings, equipment or articles of any }
\put(133.7999,-343.2162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}kind on Common Property that is reasonably likely to interfere with the peaceful enjoyment by any }
\put(133.7999,-361.5728){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}person of any Lot or Common Property other than in: }
\put(133.74,-379.8797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) proper securely wrapped parcels that will retain all odours, liquids and emissions; and }
\put(133.74,-398.2397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(ii) the receptacle or areas specified for such purpose by the Owners Corporation; }
\put(105.42,-416.5397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) not deposit any hard rubbish or flammable or noxious materials on Common Property, unless }
\put(133.7999,-434.8362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}directed by the Owners Corporation, and any Owner or Occupier found to be depositing such }
\put(133.7999,-453.1327){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}items on Common Property will be directed to remove it or the Owners Corporation will cause it to }
\put(133.7998,-471.4292){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}be removed. The Owners Corporation may recover the cost of any charges for removal of hard }
\put(133.7998,-489.7257){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}rubbish of flammable materials from the Owner or Occupier for breach of this Rule. }
\put(105.42,-508.0396){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) not burn rubbish or other materials in their Lot or on Common Property; }
\put(105.42,-526.3997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) take all reasonable precautions to keep its Lot and the Common Property fee from rodents, vermin, }
\put(133.7999,-544.5759){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}insects and other pests; }
\put(105.42,-562.9996){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) deposit all recyclable items (i.e. paper, glass and plastic bottles) in the area designated for recycling }
\put(133.7999,-581.1759){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}items by the Owners Corporation; and }
\put(105.42,-599.4797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(f) neatly break down and collapse all cardboard boxes, polystyrene and other packaging before }
\put(133.7999,-617.8364){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}depositing them in the areas designated by the Owners Corporation and under no circumstances to }
\put(133.7999,-636.1329){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}be placed down the chutes. In the event this rule is breached, and an Owner or Occupier is able to }
\put(133.7999,-654.4294){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}be identified and chute blockages occur, the Owners Corporation may recover costs associated to }
\put(133.7999,-672.726){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}clear such blockages from the responsible Owner or Occupier. }
\put(77.04,-691.1597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) An Owner or Occupier who is found responsible for dumping general waste, recycling or hard rubbish on }
\put(105.48,-709.4562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Common Property and not in the areas designated by the Owners Corporation may be charged for the cost }
\put(105.48,-727.7527){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}of any charges for removal and/or cleaning undertaken by the Owner Corporation for breach of Rule 1.5. }
\put(15,-750.8596){\fontsize{14.52}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }

\put(20.28,-78.49969){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}2. MANAGEMENT AND ADMINISTRATION }
\put(48.66,-96.85968){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}2.1. Committees and Sub-Committees }
\put(15,-103.8797){\fontsize{4.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }
\put(77.04,-117.4997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An ordinary resolution at a general meeting is required for the following decisions (which may therefore not }
\put(105.48,-135.7962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}be delegated to a Committee or otherwise): }
\put(105.42,-154.3397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) whether to appoint a manager of the Owners Corporation; and }
\put(105.42,-172.3997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) who to appoint as the Manager of the Owners Corporation; and }
\put(105.42,-190.5797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) whether to revoke an appointment of a Manager of the Owners Corporation. }
\put(77.04,-208.9997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) In the instance that the Owners Corporation wishes to or must elect a Committee to perform all or some of }
\put(105.48,-227.3563){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}its functions, it must do so in accordance with all relevant Laws and regulations. }
\put(77.04,-245.6597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) A Committee as appointed by the Owners Corporation, from time to time, may elect Sub-Committees to }
\put(105.48,-263.9562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}assist it in the performance of its’ functions. }
\put(77.04,-282.1997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(4) The Committee can delegate any or all of its functions to the Sub-Committees as permitted by Law. }
\put(77.04,-300.5597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(5) Sub-Committees must: }
\put(105.42,-318.9197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) be comprised of Members; }
\put(105.42,-337.1597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) not act outside of their delegation; }
\put(105.42,-355.5797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) act honestly and in good faith in the performance of their functions; }
\put(105.42,-373.8197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) act in accordance with the Committees instructions; and }
\put(105.42,-392.1797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) report to the Committee with respect to the performance of their functions. }
\put(77.04,-410.5397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(6) Members of Sub-Committees must vote in their capacity as members of the Sub-Committee and not as }
\put(105.48,-428.716){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Members of the Committee. }
\put(77.04,-447.0197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(7) The Committee and Sub-Committees must comply with the Rules and all applicable Laws. }
\put(48.66,-465.2597){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}2.2. Common Property and Services }
\put(77.04,-483.6797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) General }
\put(105.42,-501.9796){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) An Owner or Occupier must not do anything or permit anything to be done on or in relation to a Lot }
\put(133.8099,-520.2761){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}or the Common Property so that: }
\put(133.74,-538.6396){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) the structural integrity of any part of the Common Property is impaired; }
\put(133.74,-556.9396){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(ii) the provision of services through the Lot or the Common Property is interfered with in any }
\put(162.12,-575.2361){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}way (except temporarily as consented to by the Owners Corporation and the Owner and }
\put(162.12,-593.5327){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Occupier of any Lot affected); and }
\put(133.74,-611.8397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(iii) any support or shelter provided by that Lot or the Common Property for any other Lot or the }
\put(162.12,-630.1964){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Common Property is interfered with. }
\put(105.42,-648.4397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) An Owner or Occupier must: }
\put(133.74,-666.7997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) only use a Service supplied through meters in the Development, except in the case of }
\put(162.12,-685.1564){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}emergency or failure of supply, where safe alternative sources of energy may be used (and }
\put(162.12,-703.4529){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}without limitation, a naked flame is not a safe alternative); }
\put(133.74,-721.8197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(ii) give immediate Notice to the Owners Corporation of any accident to or fault in a Service of }
\put(162.12,-739.996){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}which it becomes aware; }
\put(133.74,-758.2997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(iii) pay on demand for Services for Common Property; }
\put(133.74,-776.5997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(iv) where its Lot is not separately metered for any Service, including and without limitation gas, }
\end{picture}

\put(162.12,-78.55969){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}electricity and/or water, then the Lot Owner will pay on demand the portion of the relevant }
\put(162.12,-99.86218){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Service and any supply charged equal to the proportion that the unit liability of its Lot has to }

\put(133.74,-136.4597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(v) not enter into any plant room, machine housing, water disposal room, electricity switch room, }
\put(162.12,-154.7562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}machinery room in or on the Common Property servicing a Lot or Common Property; }
\put(133.74,-173.3597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(vi) not adjust, interfere with or modify any Service in or on the Common Property; and }
\put(133.74,-191.4197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(vii) not use any water closets, conveniences and other water apparatus including waste pipes and }
\put(162.12,-209.7162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}drains for any purpose other than those for which they were constructed or designed. }
\put(105.42,-228.0197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) An Owner or Occupier must not interfere with or inhibit from operating any channel, ventilation }
\put(133.7999,-246.3162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}vent, duct or closure within a Lot or Common Property. }
\put(105.42,-264.5597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) Any consent given the Owners Corporation may be qualified or conditional. }
\put(105.42,-282.9797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) These rules must be given to an Occupier, not being the Owner, prior to taking up occupancy of a }
\put(133.7999,-301.2762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Lot. }
\put(105.42,-319.8797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(f) The Owners Corporation and/or Committee will from time to time issue a document titled }
\put(133.7899,-337.9357){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}‘Housekeeping Rules.’ These housekeeping rules will assist Owners or Occupiers in interpreting the }
\put(133.7899,-356.2924){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}rules contained herein in respect to how these rules should be applied on a daily basis. Accordingly, }
\put(133.7899,-374.5889){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the housekeeping rules will be binding on all Owners and Occupiers within the Development. }
\put(77.04,-392.8997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) Air Conditioning and Heating }
\put(105.42,-411.1397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) Without limiting Rule 2.2(1), an Owner or Occupier is responsible for repairing, maintaining and if }
\put(133.7999,-429.4362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}necessary replacing any air conditioning and heating equipment (including the unit, condenser and }
\put(133.7999,-447.7928){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}any items necessary to power and run the unit and condenser): }
\put(133.74,-466.0997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) that exclusively services its Lot; }
\put(133.74,-484.3397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(ii) strictly in accordance with manufacturer’s directions and requirements; and }
\put(133.74,-502.6996){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(iii) by engaging suitably qualified, insured and experienced tradespeople to do so. }
\put(105.42,-521.0597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) Where any air conditioning and heating equipment is located on, visible from outside a Lot or passes }
\put(133.8099,-539.4163){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}over Common Property, an Owner or Occupier must obtain written approval of the Owners }
\put(133.8099,-557.7128){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation before accessing that equipment. }
\put(105.42,-576.0197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) Where an Owner or Occupier wishes in to install further air conditioning and/or heating unit, they }
\put(133.7898,-594.3162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}must first obtain the Owners Corporation written approval of its position and also engage the }
\put(133.7898,-612.6729){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}buildings electrician to undertake an inspection of the power being supplied to the Lot and ensure }
\put(133.7898,-630.9694){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the wiring can take the extra load. The Owner will be responsible for payment of the cost associated }
\put(133.7898,-649.2659){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}with the inspection. An electrical certificate of compliance is required to be presented to the Owners }
\put(133.7898,-667.5624){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation confirming the additional load can be tolerated. The Owner will be responsible for }
\put(133.7998,-685.8589){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}payment of the cost associated with the inspection and certificate. }
\put(105.42,-704.2397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) Emissions of noise, vibrations or odours which, in the Owners Corporation opinion, interferes with }
\put(133.7999,-722.416){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the quiet use and enjoyment of Common Property or other Lots is not permitted. }

\put(105.42,-185.4197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) If a Lot requires an additional building induction/s per annum, the Owners Corporation may recover }

\put(77.04,-331.9397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) The Owners Corporation will and is entitled to re-coup all legal costs and all special fees/charges/levies and }
\put(105.4799,-350.2963){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}associated costs it incurs or expends in the recovery of any outstanding fees and any other costs incurred as }
\put(105.49,-368.5928){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}a result of a breach of the Owners Corporation Rules by a Lot Owner or Occupier. }
\put(77.04,-386.9597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) The Owners Corporation may commence debt recovery proceedings for recovery of outstanding fees, levy }
\put(105.48,-405.2562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}charges and other money due, against any Lot Owner of the Owners Corporation at the Victorian Civil }
\put(105.48,-423.5527){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Administrative Tribunal and the Manager and/or Committee has the power pursuant to this Rule to appoint }
\put(105.48,-441.8492){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}a lawyer to act on behalf of the Owners Corporation in relation to any such debt recovery action. }
\put(77.04,-460.2197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) The Owners Corporation may commence debt recovery proceedings for recovery of outstanding fees, levy }
\put(105.48,-478.5162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}charges and other money due, against any Lot Owner of the Owners Corporation in the Magistrates’ Court }
\put(105.48,-496.8127){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}of Victoria or any other competent Court including the Supreme Court of Victoria or the Federal Court of }
\put(105.48,-515.1093){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Australia for purposed of enforcement of recover of debts due and the Manager and/or Committee has the }
\put(105.48,-533.4058){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}power pursuant to this Rule to appoint a lawyer to act on behalf of the Owners Corporation in relation to }
\put(105.48,-551.7623){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}any such debt recovery action. }
\put(77.04,-570.0797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(4) The Owners Corporations’ right to interest does not limit any right of the Owners Corporation or: }
\put(105.42,-588.4397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) prevent the Owners Corporation recovering any amount exceeding the interest as a consequence of }
\put(133.7999,-606.7963){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}any default; or }
\put(105.42,-625.0997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) affect a Lot Owners obligation to pay the outstanding amount on the date it becomes due for }
\put(133.7999,-643.2159){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}payment. }
\put(77.04,-661.6397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(5) The Owners Corporation may, but is not obliged to, carry out any obligation of a Lot Owner that the Lot }
\put(105.48,-679.9362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owner/Occupier has failed to carry out. If the Owners Corporation elects to do this, the Lot Owner must pay }

\put(105.42,-446.9597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) performing its obligations or exercising its rights under their agreement with the Owners }

\put(105.42,-483.7997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) using Common Property that the Owners Corporation permits them to use. }

\put(77.04,-520.2197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) The Owners Corporation must not seek payment or reimbursement for a cost or charge from an Owner or }
\put(105.48,-538.5763){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}occupier that is more than the amount that the supplier would have charged the Owner or occupier for the }

\put(133.7999,-593.5363){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}appointment with the Owners Corporation, to charge a fee in relation to seeking such }

\put(105.48,-648.4362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}an amount which includes any amount that is able to be claimed as a concession or rebate by or on behalf }
\put(105.4799,-666.7327){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}of the Owner or occupier from the relevant supplier. }

\put(105.42,-703.3997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) must be claimed by the Owner or occupier and the Owners Corporation has given the Owner or }
\put(133.7999,-721.7563){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}occupier an opportunity to claim it and the Owner or occupier has not done so by the cut off fate for }
\put(133.7999,-740.0529){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the rebate or concession set by the relevant supplier; or }

\put(48.66,-123.7997){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}2.7. Owners Corporation Fees and Fund }
\put(77.04,-141.8597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) Arrears Notice Charge }
\put(105.42,-160.0997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) The Owners Corporation will and is entitled to re-coup a fee per arrears notice sent to any Lot Owner }
\put(133.7999,-178.3962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}more than a quarter in arrears. If a default letter has to be served that a fee will be chargeable by the }
\put(133.7999,-196.6927){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owners Corporation. The fee for such service is as noted in the Owners Corporation Contract of }
\put(133.7999,-215.0493){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Appointment – Additional Services or as per cost from the third party. }
\put(77.04,-233.4197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) Penalty Interest }
\put(105.42,-251.7197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) The Owners Corporation will charge interest of any amount payable by a Lot Owner to the Owners }
\put(133.7999,-270.0162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation that is outstanding 28 days after the due date until they are paid, at a rate of interest }
\put(133.7999,-288.3127){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}that must not exceed the maximum rate of interest payable under the Penalty Interest Rates Act }
\put(133.7999,-306.6093){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}1987 and in accordance with the Owners Corporations Act 2006. }
\put(77.04,-324.9797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) Maintenance Fund }
\put(105.42,-343.2797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) The Owners Corporation may establish a Maintenance Plan and Fund in accordance with the }
\put(133.7999,-361.6363){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owners Corporation Act 2006. }
\put(15.00275,-379.8727){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }
\put(20.28,-398.1797){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}3. USE OF COMMON PROPERTY }
\put(48.66,-416.5397){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}3.1. General }
\put(77.04,-434.8997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must not obstruct or prevent the lawful use and enjoyment of the Common }
\put(105.48,-453.2563){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Property by any other person entitled to use the Common Property, or use the Common Property, or allow }
\put(105.48,-471.5528){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Common Property to be used by any other person in such a manner as to unreasonably interfere with }
\put(105.48,-489.8493){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the quiet enjoyment of any person entitled to use the Common Property. }
\put(77.04,-508.1597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must not without the written approval of the Owners Corporation use for his }
\put(105.48,-526.5164){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}or her own purposes as a garden or for any other purpose, any portion of the Common Property. Any }
\put(105.48,-544.8129){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}approval may state a period for which the approval is granted. }
\put(77.04,-563.1797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) An Owner or Occupier must not use any part of the Common Property for the making of a public }
\put(105.48,-581.2958){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}announcement. }
\put(77.04,-599.6597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(4) An Owner or Occupier must always follow the direction of the Owners Corporation when using Common }
\put(105.48,-617.836){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Property. This includes all directions which are signposted in or around the Common Property. }
\put(77.04,-636.2597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(5) An Owner or Occupier must not store or keep on the Common Property or any part thereof any materials or }
\put(105.48,-654.5562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}goods (including bicycles) and other items except in designated areas if any and subject to terms and }
\put(105.48,-672.8528){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}conditions set forth in writing by the Owners Corporation. }
\put(77.04,-691.1597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(6) An Owner or Occupier must not use common property power outlets for personal use. }
\put(48.66,-709.3997){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}3.2. Accidents, Damages and Defects }
\put(77.04,-727.7597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier must not paint, finish, mark, damage, deface or otherwise alter the exterior of any }
\put(105.48,-746.1163){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Building or improvement forming part of any Lot or Common Property. }
\put(77.04,-764.4197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) An Owner or Occupier must not damage, drive nails or screws to any Common Property walls, floors, }
\put(105.49,-782.7162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}ceilings or alter a structure that forms part of the Common Property. }

\put(105.4901,-353.1022){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Manager, the Owners Corporation may take all necessary steps to make good, repair or reinstate the }
\put(105.4901,-371.4589){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Common Property at the cost of the relevant Owner or Occupier, who must reimburse the Owners }
\put(105.4901,-389.7554){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation all of its costs of doing so within 7 days of the Owners Corporation’s demand, and the Owners }
\put(105.4901,-408.0519){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation shall be entitled to recover such costs from the Owner or Occupier as a debt due. }

\put(77.04,-444.7397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier and its invitees must not consume alcohol on the Common Property except where it }

\put(139.1999,-361.5762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}installed by the Owners Corporation in the lift; and }
\put(110.76,-379.9997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) other than strictly in accordance with the directions of the Owners Corporation, which may }
\put(139.1999,-398.1158){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}include a direction to only load and deliver any goods from a rear entrance. }
\put(82.32,-416.4797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot without the consent of the Owners Corporation must not move any }
\put(110.7599,-434.8363){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}bulky goods or heavy goods, into or out of the Development except between the hours of 9.00AM and }
\put(110.7599,-453.1328){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}5.00PM on Business Days and then only when the lift protection covers have been installed. }
\put(82.32,-471.4397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) An Owner or Occupier must not hold the lift doors open and/or prevent the lift doors from closing for }
\put(110.7599,-489.7362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}any lengthy periods of time which interferes with the normal operation of the lifts. }
\put(82.32,-508.0997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(4) If an Owner or Occupier wishes to move into the Development on a weekend or after hours, that }
\put(110.7599,-526.3962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owner or Occupier must pay the costs, expenses and charges that the Owners Corporation Manager }
\put(110.7599,-544.6927){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}has determined to employ or contract staff to oversee the move to ensure the Common Property is }
\put(110.7599,-563.0493){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}protected. }
\put(82.32,-581.3596){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(5) Weekend and moves after hours can only be done after payment of the fee as approved by the Owners }
\put(110.7599,-599.6561){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation. }
\put(82.32,-617.9597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(6) The Owners Corporation, may from time to time, determine that a bond is required to be paid to the }
\put(110.7599,-636.2562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owners Corporation by the Owner or Occupier of a Lot moving in or out of the Development. }
\put(82.32,-654.5597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(7) An Owner or Occupier must take all reasonable steps to prevent any damage to any Common Property }
\put(110.7599,-672.9163){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}when moving anything over Common Property or through the Development. }
\put(82.32,-691.2797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(8) If damage is caused to any Common Property when moving anything over Common Property or through }
\put(110.7599,-709.5762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Development, the Owner or Occupier who is responsible for the move is liable for all damage, }
\put(110.7599,-727.8727){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}liability or loss arising from the moving of goods or equipment by the Lot Owner or Lot Owner’s }
\put(110.7599,-746.1693){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Occupier, including (without limitation) for any repairs or cleaning that is undertaken by the Owners }
\put(110.7599,-764.4658){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation as a result thereof and must pay on demand the costs to the Owners Corporation. }

\put(48.66,-86.83972){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}3.9. Right of Way }

\put(77.04,-233.3597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier must not use any part of Common Property for displaying any placard advertisement }

\put(105.47,-288.3162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}board or any other sign of any description on the Common Property or within a Lot where it is visible from }
\put(105.47,-306.6127){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}outside of a Lot. }

\put(48.66,-416.7197){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}3.12. Vehicles and parking on Common Property }
\put(77.04,-434.8397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must: }
\put(105.42,-453.1397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) drive in a safe and legal manner that observers all signs that are on Common Property in relation to }
\put(133.7999,-471.4362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the use of any vehicle; }
\put(105.42,-489.9796){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) park wholly within their allocated car parking space; }
\put(105.42,-508.0396){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) not park in a Lot that is not designated to them without the written permission of the relevant }
\put(133.7999,-526.3962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Occupier, a copy of which must be provided to the Manager on request; }
\put(105.42,-544.6996){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) not at any time exceed 5 kilometers per hour when on Common Property or any slower speed }
\put(133.7999,-562.9961){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}notified by the Owners Corporation from time to time; }
\put(105.42,-581.5397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) not drive in any manner that that is reckless, negligent or dangerous; }
\put(105.42,-599.6597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(f) not use or permit to be used any part of the car space allocated for use other than to park a motor }
\put(133.7999,-617.9562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}vehicle; }
\put(105.42,-636.1997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(g) only use their car parking space for the parking of registered, insured and roadworthy vehicles; }
\put(105.42,-654.6197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(h) not lease or licence the car space without the written consent of the Owners Corporation which may }
\put(133.7999,-672.9763){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}be subject to the lease or licence of the car space being granted to only another Lot Owner or }
\put(133.7999,-691.2729){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Occupier and the lease/licence must terminate on or before the lessee/licensee vacating the Lots; }
\put(105.42,-709.5197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) not sub-let any car parking space to a person who does not reside within the Development; }
\put(105.42,-727.7597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(j) not leave any unregistered or uninured vehicle on a Lot or on the Common Property; }
\put(105.42,-746.1797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(k) not load or unload vehicles other than entirely within the Development at the locations and at times }
\put(133.7999,-764.356){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}which cause minimum interference to other vehicles and other than strictly within any rules of use; }

\put(77.04,-86.89972){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(7) The cost of the Owners Corporation to tow away any vehicle will be a debt due to the Owners Corporation, }

\put(77.04,-141.8597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(8) An Occupier must not take or permit a motor vehicle or any other vehicle on Common Property that may }
\put(105.48,-160.1562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}leak or drop oil, coolant, grease, contaminants or other materials or substances on Common Property or a }

\put(77.04,-288.3197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(10) An Occupier may allow a tradesman to park in their car parking space only if the Lot Owner or Occupier: }
\put(105.42,-306.6197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) advises the Manager in advance; }

\put(105.42,-361.5197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) ensures that tradesperson’s trailers are not parked in the car park as this is not permitted; }
\put(105.42,-379.8797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) is responsible for any damage caused by the tradesperson to the Building or any property. }
\put(77.04,-398.0597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(11) Drivers must comply with all directional and speed limit signs in and around the car park. }
\put(77.04,-416.4797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(12) Drivers must exercise due care while driving in and around the car park so as not to cause danger or }
\put(105.48,-434.7762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}concern to any person or to property. }
\put(77.04,-453.1397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(13) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must keep their car spaces in a clean and tidy condition and must not litter }
\put(105.48,-471.2559){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}or pollute the car park. }
\put(77.04,-489.6797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(14) Drivers must not do or permit anything to be done which will cause a nuisance or disturbance to other Lot }
\put(105.49,-507.9762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owners or Occupiers. }
\put(77.04,-526.5197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(15) The Owners Corporation is not responsible for: }
\put(105.42,-544.6396){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) any damage to a vehicle while inside the car park or while entering or leaving the car park; }
\put(105.42,-562.8796){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) the theft of any vehicle or of any item within any vehicle parked in the car park; }
\put(105.42,-581.2397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) vehicles are parked and left in the car park as this is at the sole risk of the Lot Owner or Occupier. }
\put(77.04,-599.5997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(16) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot may only wash and clean their vehicles in the designated car wash bay (if }
\put(105.48,-617.8962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}applicable) and must seek approval of the Manager should they require the use of the car wash bay for in }
\put(105.48,-636.2529){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}excess of one hour. }
\put(48.66,-654.7997){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}3.13. Central Courtyard }
\put(77.03988,-672.8557){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Without limiting any other provision of these Rules, the following rules apply to the use of the central courtyard }
\put(77.03987,-691.2124){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}which forms part of the Common Property: }
\put(77.04,-715.6396){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) The initial opening hours for the central courtyard will be 7am to 10pm. The Manager reserves the right }
\put(105.48,-733.9962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}to modify the opening hours for the central courtyard from time to time by way of a written notice to }
\put(105.48,-752.2928){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owners and Occupiers or by placing visible signage of the amended opening hours in or about the central }
\put(105.49,-770.5893){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}courtyard or the Development.  }

\put(20.28,-322.8197){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}4. LOTS – RESIDENTIAL }
\put(48.66,-341.1797){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}4.1. Access }
\put(77.04,-359.4197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must permit the Owners Corporation to enter its Lot to enable access for }
\put(105.48,-377.7162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}external cleaning of windows and façade of building, to inspect, repair, maintain or replace any part of the }
\put(105.48,-396.0127){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Lot, the Common Property or the Services. }
\put(77.04,-414.3797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) To exercise the right under Rule 4.1(1), the Owners Corporation must: }
\put(15,-421.3997){\fontsize{4.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }
\put(105.42,-434.9597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) give at least 7 days’ Notice, except in the case of emergency, where no Noticed is required; and }
\put(105.42,-453.3197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) act reasonably to minimise any inconvenience. }
\put(48.66,-471.4997){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}4.2. Auctions }
\put(77.04,-489.8596){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must not allow any person to conduct any auction, liquidation or for sale on }
\put(105.48,-508.0959){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Lot or Common Property unless prior written approval is obtained from the Owners Corporation }
\put(105.48,-526.2122){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(acting reasonably). }
\put(48.66,-544.5797){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}4.3. Change of Use of Lots }
\put(77.04,-562.9396){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must give written notification to the Owners Corporation if they change the }
\put(105.47,-581.2963){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}existing use of the Lot in a way that will affect the insurance premiums for the Owners Corporation. }
\put(105.48,-599.5928){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Example: If the change of use results in a hazardous activity being carried out on the Lot, or results in the }
\put(105.48,-617.8893){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Lot being used for commercial or industrial purposes rather than residential purposes. Any such change in }
\put(105.48,-636.246){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}use will not be permitted by the Owners Corporation. }
\put(77.04,-654.5597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot may only change the original permitted use of its Lot: }
\put(105.42,-672.7397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) after receiving the written consent of the Owners Corporation to do so; }
\put(105.42,-691.0997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) after obtaining all necessary consents from the relevant authorities to do so; }
\put(105.42,-709.3997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) provided no other Rule will be or is reasonably likely to be breached as a consequence of the change }
\put(133.7999,-727.6962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}of use. }
\put(77.04,-746.1797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) An Owner or Occupier of a Residential Lot must not, and must ensure that the Lot is not used for any trade, }
\put(105.48,-764.2959){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}profession or business, nor permit any other person to do so, unless: }
\put(105.42,-782.6597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) the person conducting the trade, profession or business is a fulltime resident of the Lot and only }

\put(48.66,-279.9197){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}4.4. Cleaning and Repair }
\put(77.04,-298.2197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier must keep its Lot (including any garage, car park or storage cage utilised by }
\put(105.48,-316.5162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Owner or Occupier) clean and in good repair. }
\put(77.04,-334.9397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) An Owner or Occupier must ensure its car parking space(s) are free of oil, petrol and like substances. The }
\put(105.48,-353.2362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owners Corporation may clean any car parking space which is excessively stained by oil, petrol or a like }
\put(105.49,-371.5327){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}substance at the Owner's or Occupier's expense if after providing 28 days’ notice the Owner or Occupier }
\put(105.49,-389.8292){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}has failed to clean the excessive staining. The Owners Corporation may authorise a person to enter the }
\put(105.49,-408.1859){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}relevant Lot or Building on its behalf to carrying out cleaning of car spaces in accordance with this Rule. }
\put(15,-421.2197){\fontsize{4.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }
\put(77.04,-434.8397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) An Owner or Occupier must ensure that all landscaped areas visible from Common Property or which }
\put(105.48,-453.1963){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}adversely affect the outward appearance or state of repair of the Lot or the use and enjoyment of the }
\put(105.48,-471.4928){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Lots or Common Property by other Owners or Occupiers are maintained to a standard commensurate }
\put(105.48,-489.7893){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}with the standard of maintenance of Common Property landscaped areas or as reasonably directed by }
\put(105.48,-508.0858){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Owners Corporation or its Manager. }
\put(77.04,-526.3997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(4) An Owner or Occupier must keep clean all surfaces of glass in windows and doors on the boundary of }
\put(105.48,-544.6962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Lot, including any part of that glass which is in the Common Property unless; }
\put(105.42,-563.2997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) the Owners Corporation resolves that it will keep the glass or specified parts of the glass clean; or }
\put(105.42,-581.3596){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) that glass or part of the glass cannot be accessed by the Owner or Occupier safely or at all. }
\put(48.66,-599.5997){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}4.5. External Appearance of Lots }
\put(77.04,-617.9597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) Awnings, Flywire Screens, Window Furnishings }

\put(105.42,-261.6197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) use or permit the Lot to be used for any purpose which may be illegal or damaging to the reputation }

\put(105.42,-316.6396){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) use or permit a Lot to be used in a manner that would contravene any planning regulations, }
\put(133.7999,-334.9361){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}requirements or restrictions placed on the Plan of Subdivision; }
\put(105.42,-353.2397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) ensure they comply with all Lows regarding the Lot including any requirements, noticed or orders of }
\put(133.7999,-371.5362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}any governmental authority and terms (as they are applicable to a Lot Owner or Occupier) of any }
\put(133.7999,-392.8387){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}agreement under Section 173 of the Planning and Environmental Act 1987 (Vic) affecting the Lot of }
\put(133.7999,-411.1352){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Common Property; }
\put(105.42,-429.4997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) allow any part of the Lot to become unreasonably untidy, unclean or not properly maintained so that }
\put(133.7999,-447.7962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}it detracts from the amenity or appearance of the Development; }
\put(105.42,-466.3397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) dispose or permit disposal of cigarette butts, cigarette ash or any other materials from any Lot; }
\put(105.42,-484.3997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(f) make or permit to be made any undue noise in the Lot which may be heard outside the Lost }
\put(133.7999,-502.6962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}between the hours of 10PM and 8AM; }
\put(105.42,-520.9996){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(g) make or permit to be made any noise from audio equipment, music or machinery which may be }
\put(133.7999,-539.3562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}heard outside the Lot without the prior written consent of the Owners Corporation and then only on }
\put(133.8099,-557.6527){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the terms and subject to the conditions specified in that consent; }
\put(105.42,-576.0197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(h) install or authorise a person to install a locking or safety device to protect the Lot against intruders, }
\put(133.7999,-594.3162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}or a screen or barrier to prevent entry of animals or insects, unless: }

\put(162.12,-630.9163){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}materials of the Building; and }
\put(133.8035,-649.4532){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(ii) any device, screen or barrier installed is maintained in good order and repair. }
\put(105.42,-667.5797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) install additional locks or devices to the main apartment fire door that could cause the door to be }
\put(133.7999,-685.8762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}made non-compliant to the fire regulations annual audit which in any case such installation will be }
\put(133.7999,-704.2328){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}subject to obtaining the prior written consent of the Owners Corporation; }
\put(105.42,-722.5397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(j) make or permit to be made any alterations or additions whether structural or otherwise to the }
\put(133.7999,-740.8362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}exterior of the Lot and/or any Accessory Lot or any part thereof; }

\put(77.04,-316.5797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) During periods of high winds or when departing a Lot, an Owner or Occupier must: }
\put(105.42,-334.8197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) ensure all doors and windows are tightly closed, including the glazed screens to the terrace areas (if }

\put(105.42,-374.4197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) in order to minimise the likelihood of risk and damage to surrounding people or property, remove all }
\put(133.7999,-392.7162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}loose or unfixed items are also to be removed from the balcony forming part of their Lot to prevent }
\put(133.7999,-411.0728){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}items sliding into and potentially causing damage to balustrades or being thrown over the balcony }
\put(133.7999,-429.3694){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}onto other Lots or Common Property. }
\put(77.04,-447.6797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot are advised that the glazed screens may, under certain circumstances of high }
\put(105.48,-465.9762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}winds, vibrate and/or generate noise. }

\put(20.28,-502.5197){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}5. LOTS – RETAIL/COMMERCIAL }
\put(48.66,-520.9396){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}5.1. Obligations and responsibilities of Retail/Commercial Lots }
\put(77.04,-539.2397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) Without limiting any other Rule, the Owner or Occupier of a Retail/Commercial Lot (i.e. used as a }
\put(105.49,-557.5362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}restaurant, café or for other retail purpose or as commercial office space), must: }
\put(105.42,-575.9597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) apply for and obtain all necessary consents, permissions, approvals and licences to use the }
\put(133.7999,-594.2562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}retail/commercial Lot at its own costs and on conditions that are satisfactory to the Owners }
\put(133.7999,-612.5527){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation in its absolute discretion; }
\put(105.42,-630.8596){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) comply with all health, noise and other legislative requirements in carrying on the business }
\put(133.7999,-649.1561){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}from its Lot including any requirements of local council or other statutory body; }
\put(105.42,-667.4597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) at all times comply with each consent, permission, approval and licence and all Laws and }
\put(133.7999,-685.8163){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}legislative requirements in carrying on a business from the Lot including any requirements }
\put(133.7999,-704.1129){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}from local council or other relevant statutory body; }
\put(105.42,-722.4196){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) ensure trading hours and days of operation are in accordance with the relevant permits or }
\put(133.7999,-740.7161){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}otherwise as permitted by Law; }
\put(105.42,-759.0197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) not operate, nor allow access to a Commercial Lot for cleaning, between the hours of 10PM }
\put(133.7999,-777.3162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}and 7AM Monday to Sunday, without the written consent of the Owners Corporation which }

\put(77.04,-370.3997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must not affix a sign to its Lot or to the Common Property unless the sign: }

\put(77.04,-461.8997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must: }
\put(105.42,-480.3197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) make good any damage caused by the installation or removal of any sign affixed to its Lot or to }
\put(133.8099,-498.6162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Common Property and restore the Common Property to the condition it was in before the }
\put(133.8099,-516.9127){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}sign was installed; }
\put(105.42,-535.3997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) not display handwritten signs or notices which are visible from the exterior of their Lot; }
\put(105.42,-553.4597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) not display a self-standing sign such as A Frames outside the Lot boundary; }
\put(105.42,-571.8196){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) not use window displays such as for real estate listings or other display brochures unless such }
\put(133.8099,-590.1763){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}displays and brochures use a high quality cable display system and has been approved by the }
\put(133.8099,-608.4728){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owners Corporation; }
\put(105.42,-626.7797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) not affix posters, flyers or temporary signs to the internal or external of any glazing visible from }
\put(133.7999,-645.0762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the exterior of the building; }
\put(105.42,-663.3797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(f) not affix posters, flyers or temporary signs on any areas of the Common Property; and }
\put(105.42,-681.6797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(g) ensure it approved, all posters are suspended using a proprietary system in locations stipulated }
\put(133.7999,-699.9762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}on any Retail/Commercial Signage Licence or Guidelines as approved by the Owners }
\put(133.7999,-718.2728){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation. }
\put(77.04,-736.5797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) Notwithstanding any of the above, for promotions prior to commencement of trading/business, }
\put(105.48,-754.8762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}promotional material including but not limited to billboards, banners, flags and digital signage may be }
\put(105.48,-773.2328){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}permitted at the Owners Corporations discretion. }
