\put(48.66,-133.6997){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}5.4. Equipment, Facilities and Services }
\put(77.04,-151.7597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must: }
\put(105.42,-170.1197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) obtain the Owners Corporation prior written consent before an Occupier installs any }
\put(133.7999,-188.3561){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}equipment on the Owner’s Lot; }
\put(105.42,-206.7797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) obtain the Owners Corporation prior written consent before any heavy equipment is brought }
\put(133.7999,-224.956){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}on to the Owner’s Lot; }
\put(105.42,-243.2596){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) ensure all equipment installed on the Owner’s Lot must be reasonably necessary for carrying }
\put(133.7999,-258.4399){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}on the Occupier’s business in the Lot; }
\put(105.42,-276.8597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) not have any equipment that may cause any structural or other damage to the floors or }
\put(133.7999,-295.1562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}other parts of the Owner’s Lot or the Common Property or nuisance (including noise or }
\put(133.7999,-313.4527){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}vibration) to any other Lot Owner or Occupier; }
\put(105.42,-331.9397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) give the Owners Corporation at least 5 Business Days’ prior written notice before the Lot }
\put(133.7999,-349.9957){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owner brings equipment onto the Lot or the Common Property; }
\put(105.42,-368.3597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(f) obey the Owners Corporation’s reasonable requirements in relation to the routing, }
\put(133.7999,-386.536){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}installation and location of the equipment. }
\put(77.04,-404.8997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must: }
\put(105.42,-423.2597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) comply with the Owners Corporation requirements concerning the mechanical services in }
\put(133.7999,-441.5562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Building and must not do anything which might interfere with their operation; }
\put(105.42,-459.9197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) must promptly notify the Owners Corporation if it is suspected that the service in question is }
\put(133.7999,-478.0359){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}not functioning satisfactorily; and }
\put(105.42,-496.4597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) not use the water, lighting, heating and fire sprinkler systems in the Lot for any purpose }
\put(133.8099,-514.636){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}other than those for which they were constructed. }
\put(77.04,-532.9396){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must not use the water closets, drains and other apparatus for any }
\put(105.48,-551.2963){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}purpose other than those for which they were constructed and not sweep or allow rubbish or other }
\put(105.48,-569.5928){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}substances to be deposited in them. Any costs of expenses resulting from damage or blockage to }
\put(105.49,-587.8893){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}such water closets, drains, water apparatus, waste pipes and the like cause by an Owner or }
\put(105.49,-606.1858){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Occupier of a Lot will be the responsibility of the Lot Owner. }

\put(77.04,-642.8597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must not change the colour or finish to any external façade elements }
\put(105.48,-661.1563){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}which includes the colour or finish to any external floor finish outside the Lot boundary. Any }

\put(48.66,-78.61969){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}5.7. Moving and Delivery of Goods or Equipment }
\put(77.03988,-96.85608){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}This Rule must be read in conjunction with Rule 3.8. }
\put(77.04,-115.2197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) When moving goods or equipment into or out of a Lot, an Owner or Occupier must: }
\put(105.42,-133.5197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) only be made by way of the loading area designated by the Manager between the hours of }
\put(133.7999,-151.8162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}7.30AM and 6.00PM on weekdays and 10AM and 5PM on weekends or as stipulated by the }
\put(133.7999,-170.1127){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owners Corporation from time to time; }
\put(105.42,-188.3597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) ensure goods or equipment are not taken through the foyer of the Building at any time; }
\put(105.42,-206.7797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) ensure that goods or equipment are not left in the loading area or on Common Property; }
\put(105.42,-225.0797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) ensure delivery vehicles do not park within the loading area except when loading or }
\put(133.7999,-243.3762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}unloading goods; }
\put(105.42,-264.6197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) do so only at times that the Owners Corporation designates; and }
\put(105.42,-282.9797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(f) ensure that the moving of goods or any equipment is only through the designated loading }
\put(133.7999,-301.2161){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}dock. }
\put(77.04,-319.5197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) If damage is caused to any Common Property when moving anything over Common Property or }
\put(105.48,-337.8763){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}through the Development, the Owner or Occupier who is responsible for the move is liable for all }
\put(105.48,-356.1729){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}damage, liability or loss arising from the moving of goods or equipment by the Lot Owner or Lot }
\put(105.48,-374.4694){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owner’s Occupier, including (without limitation) for any repairs or cleaning that is undertaken by }
\put(105.48,-392.7659){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Owners Corporation as a result thereof and must pay on demand the costs to the Owners }
\put(105.48,-411.0624){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation. }
\put(48.66,-429.6797){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}5.8. Music }
\put(77.04,-447.7397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must ensure that music or noise from their Lot to Residential Lots in }
\put(105.48,-466.0963){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Building at all times complies with the applicable law at any point in time. }
\put(48.66,-484.6396){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}5.9. Pest Control }
\put(77.04,-502.6996){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must, at their cost, keep the Lot free from pests, including (without }
\put(105.48,-520.8759){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}limitation) cockroaches, spiders, ants, rodents and other vermin. }

\put(77.04,-594.1396){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must obtain the prior written consent of the Owners before the Lot }
\put(105.48,-612.4962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owner uses any services or equipment for cooling, heating, lighting or circulating air in the Lot other }

\put(133.8001,-170.1024){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}and is an additional charge over and above the normal Owners Corporation fees; }

\put(15,-231.9197){\fontsize{4.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }
\put(133.74,-245.4797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(iii) Between 9AM and 10AM, if any rubbish is being picked up on Sunday. }
\put(105.42,-263.8997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) take out their own bins on each garbage collection day to the bin collection area nominated }
\put(133.7999,-282.1962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}by the Owners Corporation or relevant authority and bring the bins in promptly before 10AM }

\put(105.42,-318.8597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) store all bins, bottles, cardboard/paper and any other refuse within the relevant Lot or in the }
\put(133.7999,-337.1562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}designated refuse room, (but not any car park forming part of that Lot) and must not store }

\put(105.42,-410.3597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(g) wash bins only within the Lot, excluding car spaces, or in the designated refuse wash area in }
\put(133.7999,-428.6562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}accordance with EPA regulations; }
\put(105.42,-447.0797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(h) keep the retail/commercial bin storage room and bin wash area in clean and tidy condition }
\put(133.7999,-465.1959){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}and ensure odours do not emanate outside these areas; }
\put(105.42,-483.5597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) keep all waste and rubbish in their Lot in proper receptacles and property drained before }
\put(133.7999,-501.736){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}their removal at the Lot Owner’s or Occupier’s own cost; }
\put(105.42,-520.1597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(j) immediately remove any spilled waste materials from the Common Property arising from the }
\put(133.7999,-538.4562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Occupier’s rubbish, act or omission and immediately clean any residue from the Common }
\put(133.8099,-556.7527){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Property; }
\put(105.42,-574.9996){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(k) not leave garbage or recyclable materials: }
\put(133.74,-593.2997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) on Common Property; or }
\put(133.74,-611.6597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(ii) in an area on the Owner’s Lot which is visible or detectable by smell from outside the }
\put(162.12,-629.8961){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Owner’s Lot; }
\put(105.42,-648.2597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(l) avoid unnecessary noise when filing bins; }
\put(105.42,-666.6197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(m) ensure lids on bins are securely closed at all times; }
\put(105.42,-684.8596){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(n) regularly clean all bins to precent build-up of residue of odours; }
\put(105.42,-703.2797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(o) not deposit, throw, leave or store any rubbish, dirt, dust, sweepings, waste or any other }
\put(133.7999,-721.5762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}material that is reasonably likely to interfere with the peaceful enjoyment by any person of }
\put(133.7999,-739.8727){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}any Lot or Common property other than in: }
\put(133.74,-758.2397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) proper, securely wrapped parcels that will retain all odours, liquids and emissions; }
\put(162.12,-776.5362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}and }
\end{picture}

\put(20.28,-356.1797){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}6. BUILDING WORKS }
\put(48.66,-374.3597){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}6.1. Process for Building Works }
\put(77.04,-392.7797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must obtain the Owners Corporation’s written consent prior to undertaking }
\put(105.48,-411.1363){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}any building works relating to a Lot or Services such as demolishing walls or altering the design of a Lot. }
\put(105.48,-429.4328){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Prior to commencing works under this Rule, the Lot Owner or Occupier must: }
\put(105.42,-447.7997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) if an Occupier, provide the Owners Corporation with written approval of the Lot Owner that the }
\put(133.7999,-465.9159){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}proposed works may be undertaken; }
\put(105.42,-484.2797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) provide the Owners Corporation with copies of plans, specifications, permits, consents and }
\put(133.8099,-502.4559){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}approvals, if the building works include any structural related works or works related to the Services; }
\put(105.42,-520.8796){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) if structural alterations are required, pay all costs for the Owners Corporation to appoint }
\put(133.7999,-539.1761){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}independent qualified consultants, necessary to obtain professional advice to enable it to properly }
\put(133.7999,-557.4727){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}review and determine whether or not to consent to the proposed building works including: }
\put(133.74,-575.7197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) appointment of a building surveyor; and }
\put(133.74,-594.0797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(ii) appointment of, directly or by subcontract, other experts selected by the Owners Corporation }
\put(162.12,-612.3762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}from whom the building surveyor requires input. }
\put(105.42,-630.6797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) subject to the Lot Owner or Occupier complying with all obligations under Rule 6, the Owners }
\put(133.7999,-648.9762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation will use all reasonable endeavours to act as quickly as possible to provide feedback or }
\put(133.7999,-667.2728){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}consent regarding any proposed building works; }
\put(105.42,-685.5197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) prior to commencement of any works, provide the Owners Corporation with: }
\put(133.74,-703.9397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) a copy of the relevant public liability insurance policy and certificate of currency pertinent to }
\put(162.12,-722.116){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the proposed works; }
\put(133.74,-740.4797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(ii) an estimated completion time for the works; }
\put(133.74,-758.8397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(iii) evidence or proof that any installation will not affect the external appearance of the Building }
\put(162.12,-777.1964){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}or any Common Property or Services or the fire or acoustic ratings of any component of the }
\end{picture}

\put(162.12,-78.55969){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Building; and }
\put(133.74,-97.03967){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(iv) evidence that the building works will not affect the structural integrity of the Building. }
\put(105.42,-115.0997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(f) follow the reasonable requirements and directions of the Owners Corporation; }
\put(105.42,-133.4597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(g) engage only qualified trades people, holding all necessary and current licences and insurance to do }
\put(133.7999,-151.8163){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the works, as approved by the Owners Corporation, and provide a copy of the licences and the }
\put(133.7999,-170.1129){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}insurance policy or certificate of currency for the policy to the Owners Corporation on request; }
\put(105.42,-188.4197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(h) ensure the proposed building works are undertaken in a proper and workmanlike manner and }
\put(133.7999,-206.7162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}following the drawings and specifications for the works; }
\put(105.42,-228.0797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(i) ensure that the proposed building works comply with all Laws, including obtaining the Occupancy }
\put(133.7999,-246.3762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Permit or Final Inspection Certificate when necessary; }
\put(105.42,-264.6797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(j) ensure the proposed building works are undertaken at times and in a way that minimise damage, }
\put(133.7999,-282.9762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}disturbance and inconvenience to others; }
\put(105.42,-301.2797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(k) prior to occupation, allow a building surveyor (appointed by the Owners Corporation at the cost of }
\put(133.7999,-319.6364){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Lot Owner) to inspect the completed works on behalf of the Owners Corporation and to the }
\put(133.7999,-337.9329){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}extent that they relate to Common Property or the Services, confirm in writing to the Lot Owner and }
\put(133.7999,-356.2294){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Owners Corporation, that these works are acceptable and that the Low Owner or Occupier can }
\put(133.7999,-374.5259){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}commence occupying the Lot or area for that Lot; and }
\put(105.42,-392.8397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(l) if the works to the Lot are not acceptable to the Owners Corporation on the basis that in the }
\put(133.7999,-411.1362){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}professional opinion of the building surveyor, they adversely impact Common Property or the }
\put(133.7999,-429.4928){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Services, the Lot Owner must rectify the works to the satisfaction of the Owners Corporation. }
\put(48.66,-447.7397){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}6.2. Restrictions on Building Works }
\put(77.04,-466.0997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must ensure that they and their agents and contractors undertaking the }
\put(105.48,-484.276){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}works comply with the following restrictions: }
\put(105.42,-502.6996){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) no building materials may be stacked or stored outside their Lot or in Common Property; }
\put(105.42,-521.0597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) no scaffolding may be erected on the Common Property or the exterior of their Lot; }
\put(105.42,-539.2997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) building works must be undertaken during times permitted by local Laws, as required by any }
\put(133.7999,-557.5962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}responsible Authority or the Owners Corporation; }
\put(105.42,-575.8997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) the exterior of any Building or the Lot and the Common Property must be maintained in a clean }
\put(133.7999,-594.1962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}and in a safe state at all times; }
\put(105.42,-612.7397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(e) construction vehicles and construction worker’s vehicles must not be parked on the Common }
\put(133.7999,-630.8558){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Property or in any other Lot Owner’s or Occupier’s car space; }
\put(105.42,-649.2197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(f) the method of the building operations, means of access, use of Common Property, onsite }
\put(133.7899,-667.5162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}management, building protection and hours of work must comply with the reasonable directions }
\put(133.7899,-685.8127){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}of the Owners Corporation; }
\put(105.42,-704.1797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(g) access to other Lots or the Common Property to install or maintain Services or to do any building }
\put(133.7999,-722.4762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}works required the written consent of the Lot Owner or, in the case of Common Property, the }
\put(133.7999,-740.7728){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}written consent of the Owners Corporation; }
\put(105.42,-759.0797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(h) works cannot commence before 8.30AM or continue beyond 4.30PM, although tools and materials }
\put(133.7999,-777.3762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}may be brought onsite from 8AM and taken offsite by 5PM; }
\end{picture}

\put(105.42,-96.85968){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(j) the Manager will advise which list is to be used for the transport of materials and debris, and only }

\put(48.66,-313.5197){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}6.3. Requiring notice to Owners Corporation of any Building Works to Lots }
\put(77.04,-331.7597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must not perform any renovations and/or Building Works on a Lot without }

\put(105.48,-368.4128){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Occupier of all Lots abutting the Lot to be renovated. }
\put(48.66,-386.7797){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}6.4. Damage to and Cleanliness of Common Property }
\put(77.04,-405.1397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must immediately clean and remove any dirt, debris or other rubbish }
\put(105.48,-423.316){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}resulting from the building works. }
\put(77.04,-441.6797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(4) An Owner or Occupier of the Lot must indemnify the Owners Corporation against any damage, }
\put(105.48,-459.9762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}expense, loss or liability incurred by the Owners Corporation and if the Owners Corporation makes }
\put(105.48,-478.2727){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}good any damage to, or cleans the Common Property or undertakes cleaning required as a result of the }
\put(105.48,-496.5692){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}building works, the Lot Owner or Occupier will reimburse the Owners Corporation for any cost or }
\put(105.48,-514.9258){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}liability incurred. }
\put(48.66,-533.1797){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}6.5. The Lot Owner must pay Owners Corporation costs }
\put(77.04,-551.4797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) If the Owners Corporation requires advice from an architect or other consultant concerning the proposed }
\put(105.47,-569.7762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}building works, the Lot Owner must pay on demand the reasonable fees and expenses which the Owners }
\put(105.47,-588.0728){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation incurs for seeking that advice. }
\put(105.47,-612.4915){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }
\put(20.28,-636.9197){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}7. BEHAVOUR OF PERSONS }
\put(48.66,-655.1597){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}7.1. Behaviour of Owners, Occupiers and invitees on Common Property }
\put(77.04,-673.5797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must take all reasonable steps to ensure that their invitees, do }
\put(105.48,-691.8762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}not behave in a manner likely to unreasonably interfere with the peaceful enjoyment of any }
\put(105.48,-710.2328){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}other person entitled to use the Common Property. }
\put(77.04,-728.4797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must: }
\put(105.42,-746.7797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) when on Common Property or visible from Common Property be adequately clothed and not }
\put(133.7999,-765.0762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}use language or behave in a manner likely to cause offence or embarrassment to any other }
\put(133.7999,-783.3727){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}person; }

\put(133.7999,-203.6562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}transport on the Common Property; and }

\put(133.7999,-240.2562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}or control is at all times accompanied by them whilst on Common Property. }
\put(48.66,-258.7997){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}7.2. Noise and Nuisance Control }
\put(77.04,-276.9197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot, or their guest must not unreasonably create any noise likely to interfere }
\put(105.47,-295.2162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}with the peaceful enjoyment of any other person entitled to use the Common Property. }
\put(77.04,-313.5197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) Rule 7.2(1) above does not apply to the making of noise if the Owners Corporation has given written }
\put(105.48,-331.8162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}permission for the noise to be made. }
\put(77.04,-350.0597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) An Owner or Occupier of a Lot must: }
\put(105.42,-368.4797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) ensure that no entertainment noise or any noise created by any mechanical installation is audible }
\put(133.7999,-386.7762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}outside the Lot between the hours of 10PM and 8AM (or such other hours as the Owners }
\put(133.7999,-405.0727){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation approves from time to time); }
\put(105.42,-423.4997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) not make any disturbing or irritating noises or install or use any appliance, engine, machine or }
\put(133.7999,-441.7962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}instrument which causes or may be likely to cause noise or vibration on or about the Common }
\put(133.7998,-460.0927){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Property or that can be heard or felt outside of the Lot in which the noise or vibration is emanating }
\put(133.7998,-478.3892){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}from; }
\put(105.42,-496.6996){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) not hold or permit to be held any social gathering in its Lot or on Common Property which is likely to }
\put(133.7999,-514.9961){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}cause any such noise as set out in this Rule; }
\put(105.42,-533.2997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(d) not install or operate any intruder alarm which emits an audible signal or any external speakers or }
\put(133.7999,-551.6564){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}audio amplifiers on any balcony or adjoining areas without the written consent of the Owners }
\put(133.7999,-569.9529){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation. }
\put(15.00277,-588.1893){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }
\put(20.28,-606.4996){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}8. DISPUTE RESOLUTION }
\put(48.66,-624.7997){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}8.1. Complaints }
\put(77.04,-643.1597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) Any complaint, application or request to the Owners Corporation must be addressed in writing to the }
\put(105.48,-661.336){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}secretary of the Owners Corporation or otherwise as the Owners Corporation may from time to time direct. }
\put(48.66,-679.6996){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}8.2. Grievance Procedure }
\put(77.04,-698.0597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) The grievance procedure set out in this Rule applies to disputes involving more than one of any Owner, }
\put(105.49,-716.4163){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Occupier of a Lot, the Manager or the Owners Corporation. }
\put(77.04,-734.7197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) A party making a complaint to the Owners Corporation pursuant to Section 152(1) of the Act must prepare }
\put(105.48,-753.0162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}a written statement in the approved form, and provide it to the grievance committee of the Owners }
\put(105.48,-771.3127){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation, or the Owners Corporation if there is no grievance committee, and all other parties involved in }
\put(105.48,-789.6694){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the dispute. If the person making the complaint ("complainant") does not have the address of any party }
\end{picture}

\put(15,-806.8997){\fontsize{7.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}[8200216: 28038413\_1] }
\put(105.48,-78.55969){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}involved, that person may request that the Owners Corporation or grievance committee provide a copy to }
\put(105.48,-96.8562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}that party, and if the Owners Corporation or grievance committee has the address of that party, they shall }
\put(105.48,-115.1527){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}do so within 7 days. }
\put(77.04,-136.4597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) The complainant may request, at the time of making the complaint, that the respondent attend a meeting }
\put(105.48,-154.7562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}with the complainant and the grievance committee of the Owners Corporation, or the Owners Corporation }
\put(105.48,-173.1129){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}if there is no grievance committee. }
\put(77.04,-191.4197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(4) The person about whom a complaint is made ("respondent") may respond in writing to the grievance }
\put(105.48,-209.7162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}committee of the Owners Corporation, or the Owners Corporation if there is no grievance committee within }
\put(105.48,-228.0127){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}14 working days of the date on which the respondent receives the written complaint. }
\put(77.04,-246.3796){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(5) The respondent may, at the time of receiving the complaint, request that the complainant attend a meeting }
\put(105.48,-264.6761){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}with the respondent and the grievance committee of the Owners Corporation, or the Owners Corporation if }
\put(105.48,-282.9726){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}there is no grievance committee, within 7 days and the parties to the complaint must act in good faith to }
\put(105.48,-301.3292){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}attempt to resolve the complaint within a further 7 days. }
\put(77.04,-319.8797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(6) A party to the dispute may appoint a person to act or appear on the party’s behalf at the meeting. }
\put(77.04,-337.9397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(7) If the complaint cannot be resolved within the period referred to in Rule 8.2(5), the grievance committee of }
\put(105.48,-356.2963){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Owners Corporation, or the Owners Corporation if there is no grievance committee, must notify each }
\put(105.48,-374.5928){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}party of his or her right to take further action under Part 10 of the Act. }
\put(77.04,-392.8997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(8) The process outlined in this Rule is separate from and does not limit any further action under Part 10 of the }
\put(105.48,-411.1962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Act. }
\put(15,-434.2997){\fontsize{14.52}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }
\put(20.28,-447.7397){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}9. DEVELOPER }
\put(48.66,-466.0997){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}9.1. Rules Subject to Rights of the Developer }
\put(77.04,-484.3997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) These Rules do not apply to and, are not enforceable against the Developer or its mortgagee or chargee, }
\put(105.48,-502.6962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}for so long as any of the following apply: }
\put(105.42,-521.2397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) the Developer and/or its equity partners (if any) is an Owner or Occupier; }
\put(105.42,-539.3596){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) any mortgagee or chargee of the Developer has an interest in any Lot; or }
\put(105.42,-557.7197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) the Developer and/or its equity partners (if any) is engaged in any action required to complete }
\put(133.7999,-575.896){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Development, }
\put(110.8841,-594.1925){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}where to do so would prevent, hinder, obstruct or in any way interfere with any works of any nature }
\put(110.8841,-612.5491){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}or description that the Developer their mortgagee or chargee may be engaged in or which may need }
\put(110.8942,-630.8456){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}to be carried out in order to complete construction of the Buildings and facilities comprised in the }
\put(110.8942,-649.1422){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Plan or the Development. }
\put(77.04,-667.4597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) Subject to Rule 9.1, the Developer and its equity partners (if any), its mortgagees and chargees must be }
\put(105.48,-685.8163){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}and are by this Rule, authorised by each and every Owner of each and every Owners Corporation in the }
\put(105.48,-704.1129){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Plan and by each and every Owners Corporation in the Plan to: }
\put(105.42,-722.4797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) erect such barriers, fences, hoardings, signs as it deems necessary to facilitate any works to }
\put(133.7999,-740.7762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}be carried out in relation to the Development; and }
\put(105.42,-759.0797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) take exclusive and sole possession of any parts of the Common Property as it may need to have }
\put(133.7999,-777.3762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}exclusive possession of in order to carry out any works or activities in relation to the }

\put(105.5001,-465.1823){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Developer under this Rule 9.1. }
\put(77.04,-483.6197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(4) Every Owner hereby consents to and agrees to the Developer undertaking any or all of the rights of }
\put(105.48,-501.7358){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Developer set out in this Rule without any prevention or hindrance of such Owner. }
\put(77.04,-520.0997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(5) In exercising its rights under this Rule, the Developer must act honestly and in good faith and with }
\put(105.48,-538.3962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}due care and diligence in the interests of the Owners Corporation and must have regard to the }
\put(105.48,-556.6927){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}amenity of Owners. The Developer must only exercise its rights to the extent necessary for the }
\put(105.4799,-575.0493){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}genuine Development. The Developer must not exercise its rights under this Rule to arbitrarily }
\put(105.4799,-593.3459){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}exclude the Owners Corporation or the participation of Owners. }
\put(48.66,-611.6597){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}9.2. Warranties \& Novation or assignment of contracts }
\put(77.04,-630.0197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) The Developer may at its discretion enter into contracts to supply, service, clean, maintain and/or }
\put(105.48,-648.3763){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}inspect building essentials services, other building services or functions, common areas of the }
\put(105.48,-666.6729){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Building, landscaping, or any other Common Property, and any other service or other contract or }
\put(105.48,-684.9694){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}agreements (including but not limited to agreements with neighbouring property owners) }
\put(105.49,-703.2659){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}deemed appropriate and necessary for the proper care and function of the Common Property or }
\put(105.49,-721.6226){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}which, in the Developer’s opinion, are otherwise necessary or desirable in connection with the }

\put(15,-140.4797){\fontsize{4.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }
\put(77.04,-154.0997){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}If any Rule or part thereof is found by a court of competent jurisdiction to be invalid, unlawful, unenforceable or }
\put(77.03999,-172.3962){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}void, then that Rule or part thereof shall be severed from these Rules and will not affect the continued operation }
\put(77.04001,-190.6927){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}of all remaining Rules or part thereof which are capable of separate enforcement and effect shall continue to be }

\put(48.66,-227.5397){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}10.5. References }
\put(77.03988,-245.5957){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}In these Rules: }
\put(77.04,-263.9597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) Headings and any table of contents or index are for convenience only and do not form part of these Rules or }
\put(105.48,-282.136){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}affect their interpretation; }
\put(77.04,-300.4997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) The singular includes the plural, and the plural includes the singular and vice versa; }
\put(77.04,-318.7397){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) A gender includes and genders; }
\put(77.04,-337.1597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(4) A person includes a natural person and any body or entity whether incorporated or not; }
\put(77.04,-355.5197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(5) A person includes the person’s executors, administrators, successors and permitted assigns; }
\put(77.04,-373.6997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(6) A thing includes the whole and each part of it separately; }
\put(77.04,-392.0597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(7) A reference to a law includes all laws replacing them and a reference to a statute include all regulations, }
\put(105.48,-410.236){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}proclamations, ordinances and rules issued under statute; }
\put(77.04,-428.6597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(8) A statute, regulation, code or other law or a provision of any of them includes: }
\put(105.42,-447.0197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) Any amendment or replacement of it; }
\put(105.42,-465.2597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) Another regulation or other statutory instrument made under it, or made under it as amended or }
\put(133.7999,-483.5562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}replaced; and }
\put(105.42,-501.7997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(c) Dollars means Australian dollars unless otherwise stated. }
\put(77.04,-520.2197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(9) “including” and similar expressions are not words of limitation; }
\put(77.04,-538.4597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(10) Where a word or expression is given a particular meaning, other part of speech and grammatical forms of }
\put(105.48,-556.7562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}that word or expression have a corresponding meaning; }
\put(77.04,-575.1797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(11) A provision of these Rules must not be construed to the disadvantage of a party merely because that party }
\put(105.48,-593.356){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}was responsible for the preparation of the Rules; }
\put(77.04,-611.7197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(12) If an act must be done on a specified day which is not a Business Day, it must be done instead on the next }
\put(105.49,-629.896){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Business Day; }
\put(77.04,-648.2597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(13) If two or more people are described as a party, each person is liable for their obligations and entitled to }
\put(105.48,-666.5562){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}their rights jointly and severally; and }
\put(77.04,-684.7997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(14) A reference to all or any part of a statute, ordinance or other law (statute) includes: }
\put(105.42,-703.2197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) Any rules, regulations or other instruments made under that statute; and }
\put(105.42,-721.4597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) That statute as amended, consolidated, re-enacted or replaced from time to time. }
\put(48.66,-739.8197){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}10.6. Authorisations extend to agent }
\put(77.03988,-758.1763){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Each Occupier acknowledges that any right or authority of the Owners Corporation extends to any third party that }
\put(77.03989,-776.3526){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Owners Corporation authorises to exercise that right or authority on its behalf. }

\put(48.66,-78.73969){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}10.7. Consents }
\put(77.04,-96.91968){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) Any consent or approval given by the Owners Corporation is not effective unless it is given in writing. }
\put(15,-103.9397){\fontsize{4.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }
\put(77.04,-117.5597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) Each Occupier acknowledges that it must not act of any verbal consent or approval received by the Owners }
\put(105.48,-135.9163){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation unless and until it has been confirmed in writing. }
\put(77.04,-154.2197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) Wherever the consent or approval of the Owners Corporation is required, then unless expressly specified }
\put(105.48,-172.5162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}elsewhere in these Rules, the Owners Corporation: }
\put(105.42,-191.0597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) must be given reasonable Notice of the request; and }
\put(105.42,-209.1197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) can delay, refuse or grant the consent or approval subject to any conditions which it deems fit in its }
\put(133.7999,-227.4162){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}absolute discretion. }
\put(77.04,-245.7797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(4) If the consent or approval of the Owners Corporation is given to an act, matter or thing, then the Owners }
\put(105.48,-264.0762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Corporation: }
\put(105.42,-282.3197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(a) may revoke that consent at any time, even if it was not expressed to be limited in time; and }
\put(105.42,-300.6797){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(b) did not consent to the act, matter or thing in an ongoing manner or in any way give its consent to }
\put(133.7999,-319.0363){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}any repeat of the act, matter or thing. }
\put(15.00277,-337.2727){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }
\put(20.28,-355.6997){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}11. PURPOSE OF RULES AND LAWS }
\put(48.71988,-373.9361){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}The Rules exist for the purpose of controlling, managing and administering the use and enjoyment of the Common }
\put(48.72989,-392.2326){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Property. These are binding on Owners, Occupiers and the Owners Corporation. These Rules may be amended from time }
\put(48.72989,-410.5291){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}to time by the Owners Corporation by the passing of a special resolution as defined in the Act. }
\put(48.72989,-428.8857){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}These Rules may be amended from time to time by the Owners Corporation by passing of a special resolution under the }
\put(48.72989,-447.1823){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Act. }
\put(48.72989,-465.4186){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}These Rules are binding on: }
\put(77.04,-483.8596){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) Owners; }
\put(77.04,-502.0997){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) Occupiers; }
\put(77.04,-520.4597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) The Owners Corporation; and }
\put(77.04,-538.8196){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(4) Lessees and/or sub-lessees of Lots. }
\put(14.9994,-551.0039){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }
\put(15,-563.2397){\fontsize{9.48}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n} }
\put(20.28,-575.4197){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}12. COMPLIANCE WITH RULES }
\put(48.66,-593.5997){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}12.1. An Owner or Occupier must at their cost and in a timely manner, comply with all Rules and Laws relating to: }
\put(77.04,-611.9597){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(1) Their Lot; }
\put(77.04,-630.3197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(2) The use of their Lot; and }
\put(77.04,-648.6197){\fontsize{9.962}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}(3) The use of Common Property and Services to the Building }
\put(77.04324,-666.9763){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}which include but not limited to, planning Laws, development, building or other approvals, consent requirements, }
\put(77.04324,-685.2128){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}notices and orders of statutory or governmental authorities. }
\put(48.72,-703.5197){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}12.2. An Owner or Occupier must comply with these Rules and use best endeavours to ensure that any Occupier of their }
\put(77.03989,-721.8763){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}Lot complies with these Rules. }
\put(48.72,-740.1797){\fontsize{9.99}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}12.3. An Owner or Occupier must comply with reasonable and lawful directions and Rules of use set by the Manager or }
\put(77.03992,-758.4762){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}the Owners Corporation from time to time and use best endeavours to ensure that any Occupier of their Lot, }
\put(77.03992,-776.7728){\fontsize{10.02}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}complies with all such directions and Rules of use. }
\end{picture}
